style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Company law requires the\n directors to prepare financial statements for each financial year.<a></a> Under that law the directors have elected to prepare the\n financial statements in accordance<a></a> with United Kingdom\n Generally Accepted Accounting Practice (United Kingdom Accounting<a></a> Standards and applicable law). Under company law the\n directors must not approve the financial statements unless they are satisfied\n that they give a true and fair view of the state of affairs of the company and\n of the profit or loss of the company for that period.<a></a> In\n preparing these financial statements, the directors are required to:</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;&#xD;&#xA; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:&#xD;&#xA; white\">·</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA; &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>select suitable accounting policies and then\n apply them consistently;</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:10.0pt;&#xD;&#xA; font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:&#xD;&#xA; white\">·</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA; &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">   </span>make judgements and accounting estimates\n that are reasonable and prudent; and</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA; justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA; color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">The directors are\n responsible for keeping proper accounting records that disclose with<a></a> reasonable accuracy at any time the financial position of the\n company and enable them to ensure that the financial statements comply with\n the Companies Act 2006. They are also responsible for safeguarding the assets\n of the company and hence for taking reasonable steps for the prevention and\n detection of fraud and other irregularities.</span></p><p style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">An audit involves obtaining evidence about the amounts and\ndisclosures in the financial<a></a> statements sufficient to give\nreasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a></a>\nfrom material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This includes an assessment<a></a>\nof: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the company's\ncircumstances and have<a></a> been consistently applied and\nadequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a></a>\naccounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the\nfinancial<a></a> statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>In addition, we read all the financial and non-financial information in\nthe<a></a> annual report to identify material inconsistencies with\nthe audited financial statements. If we become aware of any apparent material\nmisstatements or inconsistencies we consider<a></a> the\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">1.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><b>PRINCIPAL ACCOUNTING\nPOLICIES</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>A\nsummary of the principal accounting policies of the company, all of which have\nbeen<a></a> applied consistently throughout the year and the\npreceding year, is set out below.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Accounting\nconvention</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:StatementOnBasisMeasurementPreparationAccounts\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><span style=\"background:&#xD;&#xA; white;mso-highlight:white\">The financial statements have been prepared under\n the historical cost convention and in accordance with applicable United\n Kingdom accounting standards.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span> The financial statements have\nbeen prepared on the going concern basis as described in the Directors' Report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>In\naccordance with the provisions of FRS 1 (Revised) the company is exempt from<a></a> the requirements to prepare a cash flow statement, as it is a\nwholly-owned<a></a> subsidiary of Canary Wharf Group plc, which has\nprepared a consolidated cash flow<a></a> statement.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Turnover</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:TurnoverPolicy\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><span style=\"background:&#xD;&#xA; white;mso-highlight:white\">Turnover represents rents receivable net of VAT and\n is recognised on an accruals basis in the period in which the rents become\n due.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Interest\nreceivable and interest payable</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Interest\nreceivable and payable are recognised on an accruals basis in the period in\nwhich they fall due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Investment\nproperties</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investment\nproperties are revalued annually and in accordance with SSAP 19 (Accounting for\nInvestment Properties) no provision is made for depreciation. This departure\nfrom the requirements of the statutory accounting rules, which requires all\nproperties to be depreciated is, in the opinion of the directors, necessary for\nthe accounts to show a true and fair view. Depreciation is only one of the\nfactors reflected in the annual valuation and the amount attributable to this\nfactor is not capable of being separately identified or quantified. Surpluses\nor deficits are transferred to the revaluation reserve, unless a deficit\nexceeds previous surpluses recognised on the same property, in which case the\nexcess is charged to the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other debtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors\nare recognised initially at fair value.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective\nevidence that the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according\nto the original terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other creditors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Trade\nand other creditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current\ntax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates\nand laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet\ndate. </span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection11\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the\nrecognition of gains and losses in the financial statements and their\nrecognition in the corporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under\nFRS 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that\nhave originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions\nor events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right\nto pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as\nrecoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available\nevidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be\nsuitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying\ntiming differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance\nsheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the\ngain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial\nstatements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over\nthe period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is\nestimated that the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing\ndifferences are not expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Discount rates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been\nadopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on government\nbonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the deferred tax\nassets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><a></a><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">2.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><b>OPERATING PROFIT</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Operating\nprofit is stated after charging:</span></p><table
